NUM = COOP NUMBER
DIV = DIVISION NUMBER
ST = STATE
BEGINS = RECORD BEGINS (YEARMODY = YEAR, MONTH, DATE)
ENDS = RECORD ENDS (YEARMODY = YEAR, MONTH, DATE).  YEAR 9999 = CURRENT STATION.
LATITUDE: D  M  S = DEG, MIN, SEC
LONGITUDE: D  M  S = DEG, MIN, SEC
ELEV = ELEVATION IN FEET
